<div id="review_1243725216" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1243725216" />
    <a title="Kai" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41788524-kai"><img alt="Kai" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1573562141p2/41788524.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1243725216?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kai" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kai" href="/user/show/41788524-kai">Kai</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer13794568694913073507"><i>"Maybe there isn’t such a thing as fate. Maybe it’s just the opportunities we’re given, and what we do with them."</i><br/><br/>Stunning, heartbreaking, thrilling are just a few words to describe <i>Cress</i>. And it's not enough. This was such a good read, I had to put this book down a few times and just breath.   <span id="freeText13794568694913073507" style="display:none"><i>"Maybe there isn’t such a thing as fate. Maybe it’s just the opportunities we’re given, and what we do with them."</i><br /><br />Stunning, heartbreaking, thrilling are just a few words to describe <i>Cress</i>. And it's not enough. This was such a good read, I had to put this book down a few times and just breath. Out of fear (oh Marissa Meyer knows how to build up suspense) and relief (well at least she loves her characters enough not to kill them off one after another).<br />Cinder is brave as ever, Scarlet(well let's not spoil this), Cress is absolutely adorable(and adorkable), Thorne always lightens my sorrow-filled heart, Wolf on the other hand is the one who fills my heart with sorrow and Kai has the coolest of names. Obviously.<br />One thing I really enjoyed was reading from Iko's POV, because reading what a robot thinks and "feels" is pretty uncommon and therefore even more interesting.<br /><br />In a nutshell: possibly my favourite in the series.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/fantasticbooksandwheretofindem/" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more of my books on Instagram</a></span>

<div id="review_529142847" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/529142847" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/529142847?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=favorite-secondary-characters">favorite-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=space-travel">space-travel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=fairy-tales">fairy-tales</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=aliens-i-love-em">aliens-i-love-em</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=rabid-reads-reviews">rabid-reads-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=cover-whore">cover-whore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer529142847" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10297981788305780454"><b>Reread updates:<br/><br/><i>“The people of Luna don’t need a princess. They need a revolutionary.” <br/>Cinder furrowed her brow. “A revolutionary,” she repeated. She liked that a lot better than</i> princess.</b><br/><br/>WELP. I'm sad to say that Cress still drove me mad for the first 75% of this book, but once again, she inexplicably improved in the end. This is one series that benefits greatly from multiple POVs. <br/><br/>Onward and upwards. <br/><br/><b>THEORIES:</b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/><br/>I'm still convinced Torin is the RAT, but I'm equally convinced it's b</span></span>
  <span id="freeText10297981788305780454" style="display:none"><b>Reread updates:<br><br><i>“The people of Luna don’t need a princess. They need a revolutionary.” <br>Cinder furrowed her brow. “A revolutionary,” she repeated. She liked that a lot better than</i> princess.</b><br><br>WELP. I'm sad to say that Cress still drove me mad for the first 75% of this book, but once again, she inexplicably improved in the end. This is one series that benefits greatly from multiple POVs. <br><br>Onward and upwards. <br><br><b>THEORIES:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>I'm still convinced Torin is the RAT, but I'm equally convinced it's b/c he's brainwashed or Lunar controlled or whatever:<br><br><blockquote><i>“—stop tampering with official government property. Tampering with a royal android could result in a fine of up to 5,000 univs and six months of—Identity confirmed: Royal Adviser Konn Torin. Security override complete. Awaiting instructions.”</i></blockquote>
<br>How else would Cress know his security clearance info?<br><br>BUT. He told Cinder about the secondary chip. Hmm . . . <br><br>I'm also still convinced Wolf's elite soldier brethren are going to turn out to be a MAJOR thorn in Levana side:<br><br><blockquote><i>“I’m well aware of all that. And then she went to Paris and killed a thaumaturge and some <b>useless special operatives</b>."</i></blockquote>
<br>These guys are the equivalent of black ops soldiers, and yet this is the second time someone has called them "useless."<br><br><i>The lady doth protest too much, methinks.</i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>11/8/15:</b> REREAD. B/c WINTER. On TUESDAY. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446995256ra/16941146.gif" width="245" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*waves at Cress* <br><br><b>3.5 stars</b><br><br><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2014/02/review-cress-by-marissa-meyer.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a></b><br><br>I’ve been very up front about my love of fairy tales, and RAPUNZEL is one of the only Grimms’ Fairy Tales that has a somewhat happy ending (even if it is a little bit <i>risqué</i>). <br><br>In the original version, the prince finds Rapunzel after hearing her sing. He comes back day after day to listen to her, and, eventually, he sees the Witch and learns how to gain "entrance to her tower." <br><br>And he does. <i>Frequently</i>.<br><br>*suggestively waggles eyebrows*<br><br>Which brings us to how Witch discovers that she is no longer Rapunzel’s only visiter--Rapunzel is found to be inthefamilyway (ifyouknowwhatimean).<br><br>Anyway, Witch is so furious at Rapunzel’s “betrayal” that she cuts her hair and casts her out into the wilderness. Then she waits . . . *cue ominous music* . . . for Prince to show up, and when he does, she flings him from the top of the tower, and briers scratch his eyes, BLINDING him, when he lands.<br><br>Stuff happens and they live HEA.<br><br>CRESS by Marissa Meyer is the RAPUNZEL--based third installment of the LUNAR CHRONICLES, and while I had no urges to throw or otherwise damage books in this reading, I did have to stifle an urge to throw or otherwise damage Cress (the MC, not the book).<br><br>I’ll say up front--until around the 75% mark, Cress is downright A-N-N-O-Y-I-N-G. Fortunately, having multiple other POVs kept this from being overwhelming. <br><br>I’ve already stated that RAPUNZEL is my all-time favorite fairy tale (and has been since I was like five), so mayhap my expectations were always going to be too high. All I can say is I was dancing with glee that Meyer got the blinding (of the “prince”) part right, while simultaneously pulling out giant handfuls of hair every time Cress did a not-at-all-endearing imitation of a certain Disney character.<br><br>BUT Cinder and Kai were spot-on, and Thorne was as incorrigible as ever, so it balanced out (Scarlet and Wolf weren’t a huge part of the storyline this go-round). AND once I hit the 75% mark, Cress stopped being silly and ridiculous and started being . . . something else. I don’t know what exactly, but I didn’t hate her anymore, and that’s all that matters.<br><br>Or <i>almost</i> all that matters. <br><br>I figured out a while back that my rating system is mostly based on THE FEELS. The books that are decent, but don’t really evoke much emotion get 2 to 3.5 stars. The books that have me doing various things of a superlative nature get everything else. <br><br>Problem is, sometimes a book is pretty MEH until the very end, then BAM--THE FEELS. Suddenly, I forget all of the MEH from the front 90% of the book. <br><br>I’ve been working on that. <br><br>Which is why CRESS gets 4 stars and not 5. THE FEELS actually kicked in around the same time I stopped wanting to wallop Cress, and she was the minority (no other characters drove me batty). BUT she was the <i>main</i> character, so I didn’t feel I could in good conscience be totally swayed by THE FEELS.<br><br>I felt that Meyer wrapped up CRESS beautifully. Am I happy to be waiting another twelve months to read the conclusion? No. Of course not, but I’m still ridiculously excited to see what happens next. Especially with a nutso Lunar princess waiting in the wings. Winter is clearly C-R-A-Z-Y.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421060968i/13316940.jpg" alt="Jessica Signature" width="205" height="101" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My other reviews for this series:</b><br><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/472888024" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Glitches (Lunar Chronicles 0.5)</a>
</b><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/351598724" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Cinder (The Lunar Chronicles, #1)</a>
</b><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/472888512" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Queen's Army (Lunar Chronicles, #1.5)</a>
</b><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/403256586" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Scarlet (The Lunar Chronicles, #2)</a>
</b><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/968863200" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Fairest (The Lunar Chronicles, #3.5)</a>
</b><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/838071872" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Winter (The Lunar Chronicles, #4)</a>
</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42780417-wren-fablesandwren?shelf=physical-shelf">physical-shelf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42780417-wren-fablesandwren?shelf=05-stars">05-stars</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1843091197" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12033391660578663118">Anything I say about this book is going to do it an injustice. It was pure, it was good, it was heartbreaking and it was they most enjoyable read I have had in a long time.<br/><br/>So basically what you should do is take everything I say and just times it by a big fat ten. <br/><br/>Holy crap, okay. So the book starts out with a big bang.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803280.gif' alt='' width='350' height='196' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The gang (you know, Cinder, Scarlet, Wolf, Thorne and Iko) contacts Cress and realize she is a huge asset to their team because A: She's the one that has been hiding their spacesh</span>
  <span id="freeText12033391660578663118" style="display:none">Anything I say about this book is going to do it an injustice. It was pure, it was good, it was heartbreaking and it was they most enjoyable read I have had in a long time.<br><br>So basically what you should do is take everything I say and just times it by a big fat ten. <br><br>Holy crap, okay. So the book starts out with a big bang.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803280.gif" alt="" width="350" height="196" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The gang (you know, Cinder, Scarlet, Wolf, Thorne and Iko) contacts Cress and realize she is a huge asset to their team because A: She's the one that has been hiding their spaceship from satellites and such, B: she knows their location and has been tracking them this whole time, C: She knows all about anything they have ever done that was recorded or stored somewhere, and D: She knows all about the Queen's plans, totally geeky when it comes to computer/tablet/portscreen/whatever it's technology. <br><br><b>So they venture to go and rescue the girl with really long hair from her satellite in the sky.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803281.gif" alt="" width="350" height="197" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the whole time everyone is like, "<i>how <s>weird</s>, <s>odd</s>, <s>fragile</s>, <s>socially awkward</s>, <s>helpless</s>, <s>annoying</s>, <s>have I said weird yet</s>, <s>obnoxious</s>, <s>in-need-of-a-straight-jacket</s>, <b>special</b> is she going to be?</i>"<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803282.gif" alt="" width="350" height="192" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, let me tell you a little about our little <i>Cresent Moon Darnel</i>.<br>01. She's easily the cutest thing to ever live, Lunar, Shell or human or android or whatever else lives, walks, swims, flies or waddles.<br>02. I'm not sure who decided to portray all Rapunzel-like characters as adorable and cute and innocent and hilarious but I absolutely love it and it fits Cress <b>to a T</b>.<br>03. <b>She is dead set</b> on the fact that her and Thorne are soulmates and are going to have an epic romance because he is so selfless and honorable and wonderful and gorgeous and pure-hearted (please stop laughing, let her live in her fantasy world). He has gorgeous and wonderful going for him though, let's all be honest. Their relationship is a little like this: <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803283.gif" alt="" width="350" height="154" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After a few unfortunate events, the group gets separated: Cindy with Wolf and Jacin (<i>huh? who are you?</i> I'm probably not going to explain), Scarlet... er... elsewhere, and Cress with her beloved blind Thorne.<br><br><b>WHAT HE IS BLIND?</b> <br>Yah, I'm probably not going to explain that either.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803284.gif" alt="" width="350" height="176" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyway, a lot of the people above get trapped in the desert. I am just going to say it now: it's a very depressing read for the, er, group that gets trapped in the desert. They are down on rations, the sun is laughing at their predicament, and someone lost their shoes in the, errrr, adventure to the desert.<br><br>It's all kind of horrifying and sad and not something I ever want to put my heart through again. I read that without spoilers and I can tell you I had to count my inhales and exhales I was so nervous.<br><br><b>HOW ELSE AM I SUPPOSE TO ACT WHEN ALL MY LOVES ARE WANTED BY ALL THE CROWNS IN THE NEAR SPACE AND PLANETS AND MOONS?</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803285.gif" alt="" width="350" height="197" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh! Oh! Oh! I forgot to mention that the "evil mother" in this is <i>Mistress Sybil</i>. AND GUYS, she is <u>literally the worst</u>.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803286.gif" alt="" width="350" height="194" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm pretty sure I pulled out all my hair when her name was on the page. She ruins everything. I, UGH. No. Onto happier thoughts.<br><br>Some small things that I loved that doesn't give anything away:<br>01. Crescent's LOVE for Earth!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803287.gif" alt="" width="360" height="193" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>02. That this epic moment does happen!<br><i>even though it isn't in an epic way</i>, butttt.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803288.gif" alt="" width="350" height="177" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>03. Throne &amp; Cress because they are so <b>SHIPPED</b> I need them to <b>SAIL</b> into the <b>SUNSET</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803289.gif" alt="" width="350" height="197" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>04. How helpful Cress is to help these people she doesn't even know (well, she knows about them, but she doesn't really know them, you know?).<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803290.gif" alt="" width="350" height="197" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She literally fits so well with their team. The needs they need, she has. And she is so willing to help because she finally has a purpose in life!<br><br>05. Cress... can I just love Cress?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803291.gif" alt="" width="350" height="204" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are huge reveals, there are deaths, there are a lot of laughs, there is action, there is romance and there are three, beautiful stories woven into one huge, wonderful masterpiece. <br><br>Don't worry though, we are getting our fourth. <br>Because what do a [lunar] mechanic, [human] a pilot and a [shell] computer geek need to defeat an evil queen?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803292.gif" alt="" width="350" height="164" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>her step-daughter, the [mad] princess.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514683333ra/24803293.gif" alt="" width="350" height="140" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1422584916" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1422584916" />
    <a title="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader"><img alt="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579173421p2/43850323.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1422584916?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" href="/user/show/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader">Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★</a>

          is currently reading it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=i-love-the-cover">i-love-the-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=heroines-i-can-relate-to">heroines-i-can-relate-to</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1422584916&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1422584916" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6096644831859466665"><b>Hey, everyone! I AM BACK! </b><br/><br/>It honestly feels like such a long time since I read a book! I miss reading SO much. So I think it’s the perfect time for me to continue my reread of this series. I miss the characters already. 😊<br/><br/>•••••••••••••••••••••<br/><br/><b>THE REVIEW IS POSTED </b><br/><br/>Second Read Review : <br/><br/><i>
  <b>"I'm not an expert by any means, but I know you didn't do anything wrong today. You shouldn't tell someone you love them unless you mean it."</b>
</i><br/><br/>I think the first time I read this book, I wasn't paying much attention</span>
  <span id="freeText6096644831859466665" style="display:none"><b>Hey, everyone! I AM BACK! </b><br><br>It honestly feels like such a long time since I read a book! I miss reading SO much. So I think it’s the perfect time for me to continue my reread of this series. I miss the characters already. 😊<br><br>•••••••••••••••••••••<br><br><b>THE REVIEW IS POSTED </b><br><br>Second Read Review : <br><br><i>
  <b>"I'm not an expert by any means, but I know you didn't do anything wrong today. You shouldn't tell someone you love them unless you mean it."</b>
</i><br><br>I think the first time I read this book, I wasn't paying much attention to the characters. I think I just focused on the story ( or maybe I focused most of my attention on Wolf because I used to like him so much) so when I reread it, I felt ... like connected to all the characters and I also realized that they didn't seem what I thought they were. I mean, I felt like I knew them more after I read it for the second time, I found another personalities of some of the characters that I didn't even realize when I read it for the first time and I'm glad I reread it. <br><br>so here are the reasons why I gave this book 4 stars : <br><br><b>
  <u>The Characters</u>
</b><br><br>🌟 just like I said I felt more connected to all the characters and I used to think that Thorne only liked to flirt or joke around and oh my God, I was so wronged, he is something much more. to be honest, I personally think Thorne is quite a womanizer. oops, sorry not sorry for saying this to you guys who love Thorne but I don't hate him. how could I hate someone that made me laughing most of the time???<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397467889ra/9279495.gif" width="300" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>you know when Thorne and Cress were on dessert, I realized that Thorne is such a lovely man. he was very patient with Cress and he took care of her and he was very angry when he knew Cress was gone or taken by those people. He cared for her and it was really sweet! because honestly, I didn't really expect that from Throne. so when he got angry to Jamal, I was kind of shocked, you know and<br>I literally squealed and got excited when I read this <br><br><i>
  <b>"You're an idiot to go after her," said Jamal. "She'll already be sold, and that old man isn't going to pay for her twice. You should just cut your losses and move on. She's just a Lunar shell-she isn't worth it."<br>"if you honestly believe that," said Thorne, stowing the gun again, "then you really don't recognize true value when you see it." </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500135830ra/23302951.gif" width="300" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>in my opinion, I think Thorne already loved her even though he hadn't realized it. I just ... felt it and it was so sweet of him to protect Cress, they are just perfect for each other. *sighs dreamily *<br><br>🌟 now I'm gonna talk about Wolf. he annoyed so much in this book. I used to not have any problems with Wolf, even though I don't like him as much as I used to. I was so angry when I read this scene <br><br><b>He reached for Cinder, turning and pinning her against the wall with such force that the netscreen shook and threatened to crash to the floor. Cinder gasped, clamping both hands over Wolf's wrist as he held her suspended by her throat, feet dangling off the ground.</b><br><br>who the fuck did he think he was?!? I perfectly understood that Wolf was sad because Scarlet was taken by thaumaturge. my eyes were even teary for him but just because he was sad or probably angry, he couldn't just unleash all his emotions this way and he couldn't do that to Cinder! or anyone just because he's sad or angry. that is just not right and he made me so angry. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500138012ra/23303202.gif" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>well, I have no problems with the rest of the characters. they're all fine to me. <br><br><b>
  <u>The Plot/The Story</u>
</b><br><br>my favorite books in this series when I read it for the first time were Scarlet and Winter and I still can't say whether I like Winter or not because I'm currently reading it ( but I'm enjoying it so far ) but I can say that Scarlet is no longer my favorite and Cress is definitely better than Scarlet. I enjoyed reading Cress more and this series gets better and better, which is really awesome! <br><br><b>
  <u>The Romance</u>
</b><br><br>Person : so ... how did you think about the romance?<br>me : asdfghjkldhsfghdsfhjsdghjsgddfhdg<br>Person : um ... what? I don't think I heard you well<br>me : *inhales* THE ROMANCE WAS EPIC AND REALLY SWEET AND I HAVE NO WORDS HOW TO DESCRIBE HOW SWEET IT WAS. *exhales*<br><br>I'M GONNA READ WINTER NOW SO BYE BYE *blows kisses*<br><br><s>
  <b>REVIEW TO COME TOMORROW.</b>
</s><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><s>
  <i>
    <b> I WILL REREAD THIS SERIES THIS YEAR</b>
  </i>
</s><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br>First Read Review : <br><br>I just finished this book and i really loved it <br>This book was so romantic and so action <br>I love everything about this book,everything was so perfect.<br>The characters,the plot,the story and everything were so amazing<br>I really need the 4th book!!!<br>I hope the 4th book won't disappoint me :D <br>I highly recommend these series for everyone that love YA fantasy-romance because these series BLEW MY MIND!</span>

Thorne is the charming scoundrel pilot (still picture Han Solo) . . . I care about the characters and what happens to them. I enjoy the relationships. It might be kinda chees</span>
  <span id="freeText5230016866635310523" style="display:none">Cress is Rapunzel . . . Scarlet is Red Riding Hood . . . Cinder is Cinderella . . . Wolf is the not so Big Bad Wolf . . . Thorne is the charming scoundrel pilot (still picture Han Solo) . . . Iko is the quirky droid<br><br>A cross between fairy tales and Star Wars - really, Star Wars fans might hate me for blasphemy, but I really do keep thinking about it!<br><br>I like this series - it is very entertaining! I care about the characters and what happens to them. I enjoy the relationships. It might be kinda cheesy from time to time, but I love me some brie! :)<br><br>Note on Thorne and Cress . . . <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ per Wikipedia from the Rapunzel story regarding the prince who loves her: "he leaps from the tower in despair and is blinded by the thorns below"  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> it all makes so much sense now!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458835137i/18537220.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_674889212" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/674889212" />
    <a title="Natalie Monroe" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6688207-natalie-monroe"><img alt="Natalie Monroe" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339730817p2/6688207.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/674889212?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie Monroe" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie Monroe" href="/user/show/6688207-natalie-monroe">Natalie Monroe</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=bubbling-under-5-stars">bubbling-under-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=kick-ass-heroines">kick-ass-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=pants-are-snowmen-and-they-are-june">pants-are-snowmen-and-they-are-june</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=fearless-protagonists">fearless-protagonists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=laugh-out-loud-humor">laugh-out-loud-humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=pleasantly-surprised">pleasantly-surprised</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6688207-natalie-monroe?shelf=girl-squad">girl-squad</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer674889212" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8964717764539240741"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"Because if there was one thing Cress knew about heroes, it was that they could not resist a damsel in distress. <br/><br/>And she was nothing if not in distress."</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403679687ra/10128168.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Cress isn't the type of character I usually like.</b> She's naive, obsessed with grand destined love, frets about not having been kissed while possibly dying. <br/><br/>Yet strangely all these things only serve to make her <b>more endearing and charming.</b> In my first read of the Lunar Chronicles, Cress was the book that made me fall head-over-heels i</span>
  <span id="freeText8964717764539240741" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Because if there was one thing Cress knew about heroes, it was that they could not resist a damsel in distress. <br><br>And she was nothing if not in distress."</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403679687ra/10128168.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cress isn't the type of character I usually like.</b> She's naive, obsessed with grand destined love, frets about not having been kissed while possibly dying. <br><br>Yet strangely all these things only serve to make her <b>more endearing and charming.</b> In my first read of the Lunar Chronicles, Cress was the book that made me fall head-over-heels in love with the series. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13206760.Scarlet__The_Lunar_Chronicles___2_" title="Scarlet (The Lunar Chronicles, #2) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Scarlet</a> was lovely; Cress triggered fangirl mode.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Captain?"<br><br>"Yeah?"<br><br>"Do you think it was destiny that brought us together?"<br><br>He squinted and, after a thoughtful moment, shook his head. "No. I'm pretty sure it was Cinder.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500951080ra/23399132.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Meyer just <i>gets it</i>, how to create sweet characters without making them annoyingly optimistic, naive characters without making them ignorant. It's like that in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18584855.Heartless" title="Heartless by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Heartless</a>, too.<br><br>It helps that Cress is a Rapunzel retelling, and Meyer likely drew inspiration from Disney's Tangled as well. Cress has been trapped on a satellite nearly all her life, being Queen Levana's (unwilling) hacker. After she's rescued, she's amazed at the sights and smells of Earth while still being her adorable, brave self. Thorne is slightly egoistic and never fails to deliver a witty line even in the company of enemies. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500951080ra/23399131.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their romance beats Scarlet/Wolf's on the squeal level. It's slowly fleshed out and very well-developed. Cress builds up an unhealthy idealistic image of Thorne at first, but she slowly begins to get to know the real Thorne and really falls in love with him in the process. Thorne, in turn, doesn't take advantage of Cress's initial starstruck state and even reminds her that he's the first guy she's ever met so she should reevaluate her true feelings. <br><br>And that fucking promise. You know what I'm talking about. ;)<br><br>If I have one complaint, it's Cinder. (It's always fucking Cinder, which destroyed the first book for me and almost made me give up on the series) <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Why didn't she just straight out tell Kai she's princess Selene when she was kidnapping him? A lot of unnecessary drama and misunderstanding could've been avoided if she did, and she's planning to start a revolution anyway so it doesn't matter who finds out. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The writing is nice. Still not the most amazing thing I've ever read, but gets the job done. There aren't metaphors that change the way I look at the world. This series is mostly about the characters—Scarlet and Wolf, Cinder and Kai, Cress and Thorne, always. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Still lowkey mad Scarlet and Wolf didn't get much bonding time before being ripped apart. Yet Cinder and Kai, aka most boring couple in the world, get time together. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Best book of the series.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500951080ra/23399133.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8964717764539240741" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText11392201362661315069" style="display:none"><b>*Spoilers Ahead*</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>And at last I see the light<br>And it's like the fog has lifted<br>And at last I see the light<br>And it's like the sky is new<br>And it's warm and real and bright<br>And the world has somehow shifted<br><br>All at once everything is different<br>Now that I see you<br><br>Now that I see you<br>-Tangled (2010)</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596174969ra/29890200.gif" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The time has come</b> for the ultimate fangirling episode. The book which <b>
  <u>cemented</u>
</b> my relationship with this series. This is so amazing i mean it's my favorite in the series and Cinder ... I know i have already adopted so many many children but PLEASE BE MY DAUGHTER.<br><br>Where do i even begin? Cress Of course!<br><br>So Cress.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596175503ra/29890211.gif" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>CRESS.<br><br>CRESS.<br><br>CRESS.<br><br>This book holds my heart and it has everything i want in an adventure and so many things happen in this book gahhhhhhh!!! The drama, the plot twists, the romance, the epic battles, heists, and most importantly Carswell Thorne. The DRAMA MY DUDES THE <b>
  <i>DRAMA</i>
</b>.<br><br><b>
  <u>Let's do this thing.</u>
</b><br>● <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Even in the future, there are damsels in distress…</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>● Starting with the obvious .... Cress!!<br>● The shy girl, the fan girl, the hopeless romantic, the imaginative dreamer. Socially inept and very, very prone to blush!<br>● In all my years reading YA and finding the sarcastic, whip smart, kick butt heroines (whom I love) I had never encountered, a wee little girl, who’s quiet, smart but not at all great with the whipping of the smarts. Then I found Cress and just …<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596176404ra/29890247.gif" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● I may not be a tech-savvy genius, but I am definitely the kind of person to make up crazy fantasies and talk to myself! And they would most certainly be about a very swoony Vampire! (i dream about a very very particular vampire)<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596176404ra/29890248.gif" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● I am so glad that along with i-am-gonna-kick-your-butt heroines we also have still-finding-the-courage heroines.<br>● And now onto our glorious returning characters ...<br>● CINDER<br>● aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa<br>● aaaaaaaaaaahhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhh<br>● la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la la<br>● LORDDDDDD<br>● LORDY LORDY LORD<br>● HOW IS IT THAT WITH EVERY BOOK I FALL EVEN MORE IN LOVE WITH HER SARCASM AND HER MECHANIC THINGY?!<br>● I ADORE EVERYTHING THAT HAS TO DO WITH CINDER.<br>● <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You said yourself that the people of Luna need a revolutionary.” She lifted her chin, holding his gaze. “So I’m going to Luna, and I’m going to start a revolution.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>● She is my daughter people.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596178154ra/29890347.gif" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● And KAI<br>● WORLD STOP HURTING HIM.<br>● With Levana hovering over his shoulder you can’t blame him if he is a little down in the dumps! Especially since he still has feelings (though he “denies” them) for Cinder and basically the whole world and moon are trying to arrest her!<br>● MY POTATO<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596178154ra/29890348.gif" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● His sass however, is always spot on:<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Have you given any thought to your wedding vows?”<br>Kai snorted. “Delete anything that has to do with love, respect, or joy, and I’ll sign on the dotted line.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>● Of all the characters Scarlet was the least focused on in this book because *things* happen...<br>● #feelssssssssssssssssssssss<br>● poor gurl :(<br>● AND WOLF IS TEN TIMES BROODIER BECAUSE OF THE "THINGS"<br>● He goes through a lot of emotions too and takes a back seat in this one. I do love all his scenes though, I can’t get enough of my little wolf!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596178154ra/29890349.gif" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● Iko Iko Iko<br>● IKO<br>● IKO ALL DAY. She has the biggest personality and heart, despite only being a small chip!<br>● <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The other girl, Iko, cupped her chin with both hands. "This is so much better than a net drama.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>● Her sass though #goals.<br>● Jacin ... meh ¯\_(ツ)_/¯<br>● don't care 'bout you my lad.<br>● and *ahem* Thorne.<br>● T<br>● H<br>● O<br>● R<br>● N<br>● E<br>● <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Seeing that smile, Cress melted. Every. Time.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>● me too Cress me too.<br>● CRESS GET THE HELL OUT OF THE WAY CAUSE THORNE IS MINE.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596178154ra/29890350.gif" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● I can’t help it! He is just everything that I needed from a fictional love interest. Funny. Suave. Foolish. Heroic yet criminalistic.<br>● ⚠️⚠️⚠️coherent thoughts not found<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1596183867i/29890906._SX540_.png" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● *sighs*<br>● His heroics are put on full display in this book, on his journey with Cress. His humour, swooniness and overall gorgeousness are always on display.<br>● And this:<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Wha—where'd she go?" Thorne's voice came to her through the screen.<br>"Honestly, Thorne." A girl. Linh Cinder? "Do you ever think before you speak?"<br>"What? What did I say?"<br>" 'Is that all hair?' "<br>"Did you see it? It was like a cross between a magpie nest and ball of yarn after it's been mauled by a cheetah."<br>A beat. Then, "A cheetah?"<br>"It was the first big cat that came to mind.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>● I just can’t okay. The feels are too much when it comes to Thorne.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596178154ra/29890351.gif" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● and Levana is such a prefect villain i just LOVE TO HATE HER.<br>● THE RAMPION CREW GUYS!!!!!!!!!!!!<br>● how is everyone not screaming?!<br>● I mean:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1596183867i/29890907.jpg" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● *sighs*<br>● And the ships.<br>● Dagummit.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1591635783i/29615436.jpg" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● We have a lot of <b>Cresswell</b>. <br>● <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Captain,” she murmured.<br>“I think I’m in love with you.”<br>An eyebrow shot up. She counted six beats of his heart before, suddenly, he laughed.<br>“Don’t tell me it took you two whole days to realize that. I must be losing my touch.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> NO THORNE IT TOOK NANOSECONDS TO FALL IN LOVE WITH YOU.<br>●<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Captain?”<br>“Yeah?”<br>“Do you think it was destiny that brought us together?”<br>He squinted and, after a thoughtful moment, shook his head. “No. I’m pretty sure it was Cinder.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>THIS DUDE THIS.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1596183867i/29890908._SY540_.jpg" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>●<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“But you’re a prisoner,” said Thorne.<br>“I prefer damsel in distress,” she murmured.<br>One side of Thorne’s mouth quirked up, into that perfect half smile he’d had in his graduation photo. A look that was a little bit devious, and all sorts of charming.<br>Cress’s heart stopped, but if they noticed her melting into her chair, they didn’t say anything.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I WOULD HAVE DIED.<br>●<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“How are your eyes?” she asked.<br>“Well, I’ve been told they’re dreamy, but I’ll let you decide for yourself.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>DREAMY, SWOON WORTHY, PERFECT!! <br>●<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“She loved him more than ever. And not because she’d scoured file after file of reports and summaries and data and photographs. Not because he was the dreamy, untouchable Carswell Thorne that she’d imagined kissing on the banks of a starlit river while fireworks exploded overhead and violins played in the background. Now he was the Carswell Thorne who had given her strength in the desert. Who had come for her when she was kidnapped. Who had kissed her when hope was lost and death was imminent.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>● *ddddddddeeeeeeeeeeeeeaaaaaaaaaaaaaadddddddddddddddd*<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1596183867i/29890909._SY540_.jpg" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>● And then we have Wolflet.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Aaaaw,” squealed Iko. “Did Wolf just say he loves Scarlet? That’s so cute!”<br>Scarlet cringed. “He did not – that wasn’t -” She balled her fists against her sides. “Can we get back to these soldiers that are being rounded up, please?”<br>“Is she blushing? She sounds like she’s blushing.”<br>“She’s blushing.” Thorne confirmed, shiffling the cards. “Actually, Wolf is also looking a little flustered -”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>● awwwwwwwwwwwwwww<br><blockquote>
  <b>

<span id="freeTextContainer6928242305320612600">Okay so I'm going to be honest, I was a little bored with this one early on when it was just mostly Cress and Thorne wandering around the desert, but then HOLY CRAP this book got good!<br/>There was so much going on in this and it was so exciting and I just loved the way all the characters' story lines were all tied in with each other, and literally just this story is so gripping. I love it. I love all of the characters. Their each so unique and wonderful and flawed and beautiful and swing all of the</span>
  <span id="freeText6928242305320612600" style="display:none">Okay so I'm going to be honest, I was a little bored with this one early on when it was just mostly Cress and Thorne wandering around the desert, but then HOLY CRAP this book got good!<br />There was so much going on in this and it was so exciting and I just loved the way all the characters' story lines were all tied in with each other, and literally just this story is so gripping. I love it. I love all of the characters. Their each so unique and wonderful and flawed and beautiful and swing all of them together and how they interact is like watching a perfect symphony. I don't even know if I'm being coherent right now, but I really don't care. This book punched me right in the feels.<br />I'm not going to spoil anything but it was also kind of heartbreaking at times, and I'm really anxious for a certain person who's still apart from the group. She needs to catch a break, like seriously. <br />And I am SO intrigued by Winters character! She's like space Luna and I love it. We only got a couple glimpses of her here, but I can't to read Winter now and get MORE! <br />Anyway, rambling over. I loved this. On to the next one!</span>

<div id="review_2584767336" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2584767336" />
    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2584767336?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2584767336" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1761472253637072802"><i>“I promise, I will not let you die without being kissed.” </i> <br/><br/>Story 🌟🌟🌟<br/>Once upon a time deep deep in the sky between lunar and earth there lived a girl, a human shell who was trapped there. She was forced to work for the evil lunar queen, help to destroy and conquer the earth. But all the time alone made the little girl curious for the enemy she was forced to spy on. <br/>She was fascinated by it. The music, the people, the news. <br/>With the years passing by her hair grew longer and longer. <br/>She was dreamin</span>
  <span id="freeText1761472253637072802" style="display:none"><i>“I promise, I will not let you die without being kissed.” </i> <br /><br />Story 🌟🌟🌟<br />Once upon a time deep deep in the sky between lunar and earth there lived a girl, a human shell who was trapped there. She was forced to work for the evil lunar queen, help to destroy and conquer the earth. But all the time alone made the little girl curious for the enemy she was forced to spy on. <br />She was fascinated by it. The music, the people, the news. <br />With the years passing by her hair grew longer and longer. <br />She was dreaming about a handsome hero that would save her. <br />And then one day someone came. He was handsome, maybe even a real hero with a gorgeous grin that made the knees of many girls weak. <br />He did not come on a white horse, but on a space ship with his weird outcast crew. <br />But then - well, you need to read the book to know what happened then. <br />And you know what? It was a hell of an adventure. <br />So much action, so many fights, betrayals, plot twists and sweet, cute love. <br />I really liked this book even though I think it wasn’t as good as the second one. <br /><br />Character 🌟🌟🌟🌟<br />My favorite character in this book was definitely Cress. She was such a smart, clever and lovely girl. She always wanted to be the damsel that was saved by the hero. <br />But then she realized, a hero is great don’t get me wrong, but she should and she could save herself. Because even though many of the stories go like this - the best stories are the ones where there is a smart girl that knows how to save herself - or at least knows that she needs to try. <br />Next to Cress there will be my all time cinnamon roll and baby Cresswell Thorne. <br />Absolutely gorgeous, handsome, funny and so adorable. The way he knows that he’s not a perfect guy, not a hero, but still tries to protect and help his friends. It was so heartwarming. Ugh, I love him so much. <br />Also right after Thorne there is my baby wolf ♥️ his love for Scarlet is everything and it’s so freakin cute. <br />Also I loved Iko, her sarcasm and her absolutely lovely character. One of the best side characters I’ve seen in a while (I’m thinking about Kenji from Shatter me😍). <br />Cinder had a strong character development in my opinion. First of all she realized she is stronger that she thought. Also she knew when she lost and when she needed to let go. It was really mature and really royal of her. <br />I really liked that she was getting stronger with her lunar gifts and that she knew how to plan things but also how it was time to trust other people with their experiences and ideas. <br />All in all I really liked the characters of the book. <br /><br />Relationships 🌟🌟🌟<br /><i>“Maybe there isn’t such a thing as fate. <br />Maybe it’s just the opportunities we’re given, and what we do with them. <br />I’m beginning to think that maybe great, epic romances don’t just happen. <br />We have to make them ourselves.” </i> <br />Like I said in my review for the first and second book: there is always this heartwarming cute and lovely romance that will make your heart ache and warm and ugh. <br />And in this one there will be one couple you’ll ship like crazy - Thorne and Cress. Those two are the cutest. They’re the perfect team, they harmonize well and they protect each other no matter what. I really really liked them. ♥️<br />Also there was Scarlet and my baby boy wolf. The whole alpha family thing was so freaking cute and I couldn’t love it more that I did. <br />All the other romance in this book - meh. <br /><br />Writing style 🌟🌟🌟<br />Well, like I said in the other reviews, I liked Meyers writing. It’s entertaining, but it’s nothing extraordinary or special. <br />It’s good, it’s sometimes funny, but it’s all in all a normal nice writing. <br />Although we had many POVs in the first and second book, I have the feeling that we get more and more POV with every book the author adds to the series. <br /><br />All in all I’m satisfied with this book and will read the last and final book of the series immediately. 🎈</span>
  <a data-text-id="1761472253637072802" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1231424351" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1231424351" />
    <a title="Dorreh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22599584-dorreh"><img alt="Dorreh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565727363p2/22599584.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1231424351?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dorreh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dorreh" href="/user/show/22599584-dorreh">Dorreh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1231424351" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17806021561156402304">Well I probably want to start with the fact that I didn't give this book the 5 full stars I gave the other two books before this one. It's not a matter of liking this book less, because I didn't, I loved it just as much as the other two, only this one had some minor mishap that made it slightly less appealing. <br/><br/>For starters the book had a relatively slower pace than the other two, and when it's a matter of comparison, this point stands out in an authors style of writing. This slow pace in turn le</span>
  <span id="freeText17806021561156402304" style="display:none">Well I probably want to start with the fact that I didn't give this book the 5 full stars I gave the other two books before this one. It's not a matter of liking this book less, because I didn't, I loved it just as much as the other two, only this one had some minor mishap that made it slightly less appealing. <br /><br />For starters the book had a relatively slower pace than the other two, and when it's a matter of comparison, this point stands out in an authors style of writing. This slow pace in turn lengthened the book to about 500 something pages. Now under normal circumstances I would have relished the vivid detailing of the book, however, in this case it wasn't as mesmerizing. This was mostly because we are already familiar with the ideas and settings of this story as a whole. This was a huge deal for me, because slow pace and a long way to go, make me bored. Many parts of the book were so full of intrigue I simply couldn't stop, but at other times the feeling disappeared and was replaced by a sort of detachment. <br /><br />But that makes an unfair complaint, because compared to so many books, this one is so great. The main issue for me was that its predecessors were so good that the slight difference in this book made a huge difference for me!<br /><br />So now to all the great things about this book. First of all it was so entertaining! All the characters, all the plotting and moving and incredible amounts of action. I think I was still majorly hooked on scarlet and wolf, so all through out the book, I was just waiting for the parts that wolf and Scarlett story is told. I also have a peculiar yet healthy curiosity about princess winter, I mean like literally not being able to wait to see what her story is. So yes, that indirectly means I'm so looking forward to the fourth installment. <br />I'm going to emphasize the negativity that I initiated this review with is only to explain the one missing star in my rating, because otherwise I did love this book, and would recommend it to everyone who liked the previous two.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17806021561156402304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3589023473" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3589023473" />
    <a title="Sofia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/114413220-sofia"><img alt="Sofia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606141536p2/114413220.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3589023473?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sofia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sofia" href="/user/show/114413220-sofia">Sofia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114413220-sofia?shelf=enough-with-the-darn-rebellion">enough-with-the-darn-rebellion</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114413220-sofia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114413220-sofia?shelf=gary-stu">gary-stu</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114413220-sofia?shelf=multiple-perspectives">multiple-perspectives</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114413220-sofia?shelf=intriguing-male-species">intriguing-male-species</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114413220-sofia?shelf=otp">otp</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114413220-sofia?shelf=that-one-character-i-hate">that-one-character-i-hate</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114413220-sofia?shelf=mary-sue">mary-sue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114413220-sofia?shelf=strong-female-protagonist">strong-female-protagonist</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114413220-sofia?shelf=tries-to-be-sad">tries-to-be-sad</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3589023473" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5494713450703101929">Yep. It definitely got better.<br/><br/>This was my favorite of the Lunar Chronicles. It was so sweet and personal, while keeping up the action-packed plot. Each time Thorne and Cress popped up, I devoured every word. They're my cinnamon rolls. <br/><br/>I had one big problem, however.<br/><br/>Wolf. I hate him. <br/><br/>He spent a good chunk of this book unconscious, which I felt was deserved. And then, when he wakes up, he has a temper tantrum because "his alpha was missing," he rips his stitches, and he puts Princess Selene in a c</span>
  <span id="freeText5494713450703101929" style="display:none">Yep. It definitely got better.<br /><br />This was my favorite of the Lunar Chronicles. It was so sweet and personal, while keeping up the action-packed plot. Each time Thorne and Cress popped up, I devoured every word. They're my cinnamon rolls. <br /><br />I had one big problem, however.<br /><br />Wolf. I hate him. <br /><br />He spent a good chunk of this book unconscious, which I felt was deserved. And then, when he wakes up, he has a temper tantrum because "his alpha was missing," he rips his stitches, and he puts Princess Selene in a chokehold. And then he proceeds to spend the rest of the day howling in a corner like the useless character he is. <br /><br />Maybe I wouldn't have minded this if he actually treated Scarlet like a person and not like some "alpha" thing he's supposed to be proud of. Or if they had known each other for longer than a month. <br /><br />When they break into the palace, he's STILL MOPING and refuses to even try to act like he's enjoying the party. They're supposed to blend in, and yet he won't even attempt to look any more like an actual human being. He's too busy "mourning Scarlet." Pleeease. Wolf needs two things. Therapy and a class on anger management. <br /><br />Besides that... <br /><br />I loved Cress and Thorne and Cresswell with all of my shriveled heart. Cress is adorably naive (did I mention that Rapunzel is my favorite fairy tale), Thorne is the perfect combination of sarcastic and supportive, and together - *cries* *swoons* PERFECTION. <br /><br />Oh, and Kai was officially elevated to Cinnamon Roll Status. Because Wolf dropped. Kai's like those slightly stale cinnamon rolls you get from the grocery store bakery in a plastic box... while Cress and Thorne are fresh, warm, sticky ones. Sorry for the food analogy, I couldn't help myself. <br /><br />The plotline itself was entirely too convenient. They all happen to land up in the same obscure African town JUST BY CHANCE. Which I find hard to believe. But I'm going to stop being skeptical and just enjoy this magnificence.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5494713450703101929" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('d32B3hiO572swzGHGcWIY0PcpdAttAz6l9lvPjmcXup3CNP/D6MX3ioLhInmY0Hd3HgNJhjhBlFL+yxSYnSeew==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IyZJsgyET5rdKKyNlM+KGRbDKHS/pnU8jta/LMQnTjsjUxuTG6m/+VvgGYNraUOniWeAgorzf5dS9PxAn8+Oqg==')})
  }
//]]>
